01:33:39","updatedTime":"2021-07-15 01:33:39","title":"Remote work is expanding rapidly beyond typical white-collar worker industries","link":"https://www.businessinsider.com/remote-job-postings-rise-construction-healthcare-logistics-says-linkedin-2021-7","description":"<figure>\n\t<img src=\"https://i.insider.com/60eee920a8d8c00019b0312d?format=jpeg\" alt=\"Designer works at office desk.\" height=\"5109\" width=\"6812\" charset=\"\">\n<figcaption>Back offices roles in construction and logistics are increasingly going remote.\n<p class=\"copyright\">Cravetiger via Getty.</p>\n</figcaption>\n</figure><ul class=\"summary-list\">\n<li><strong>The number of remote roles posted online has risen by as much as 19 times for some UK sectors, according to LinkedIn.</strong></li>\n<li><strong>Remote roles in transport, construction, and retail have grown significantly.</strong></li>\n<li><strong>The rise has been fueled by growing acceptance of remote work, as well as an adoption of technology. </strong></li>\n<li id=\"recirc\"><a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/?hprecirc-bullet\">See more stories on Insider&#39;s business page</a>.</li>\n</ul><p>The number of remote job roles being advertised has risen, making remote work a possibility for more workers.</p><p>But not all of these are in industries traditionally associated with remote work, with workers in transportation, retail and construction increasingly being offered a remote option. </p><p>LinkedIn&#39;s <a href=\"https://www.linkedin.com/pulse/remote-work-job-listings-rise-hiring-uk-recovering-rapidly-morrin/\">UK Workforce report</a> analyzed job postings on the site between June 2020 and June 2021. A job was classed as remote if it was explicitly labelled as such, or contained key phrases like &#34;work from home.&#34;</p><p>It generally found that the number of remote roles has risen across the board. </p><p>Unsurprisingly, white-collar industries more traditionally associated with working from home have seen levels of postings rise since June 2020. </p><p>As a sector, IT and software saw a 5.5x year-on-year increase in the overall percentage of available remote roles - one in five IT roles are now advertised as remote. In June 2020, 1.6% of finance roles were advertised as remote, which grew to 10.9% in 2021, a 7x year on year increase.</p><p>The largest increase however has been seen among transportation and logistics roles, which has seen remote roles rise 18.5x, to 5.6%, compared to June 2020 levels of 0.3%. </p><p>Other industries more traditionally associated with in workplace roles have seen an increase. Retail rose 11.6x, while construction experienced a 5.7x increase. </p><p>Healthcare, education and entertainment and travel also saw remote postings rise by 6.7x, 5.4x and 9.3x respectively. </p><h2><strong>The pandemic has introduced many to the idea of working remotely</strong></h2><p>&#34;Traditional office roles have naturally found it easier to pivot to a remote working style. From software engineers to media and communications professionals, workers across a myriad of sectors have shown they can work remotely if they need to by leaning on technology to stay connected,&#34; said Mariano Mamertino, senior economist, EMEA at LinkedIn. </p><p>&#34;But even in a field like healthcare, where in-person care is the very essence of many jobs, remote work is making surprising inroads.&#34;</p><p>Roles in project management, legal teams, blog editors and roles in utilization review are examples of some of the support functions that don&#39;t have to be done onsite, adds Mamertino.</p><p>The pandemic has also opened workers&#39; and executives&#39; eyes to the benefits of working from home in industries where they previously would not have, said Janine Chamberlin, UK country manager at LinkedIn.</p><p>&#34;Over the past year, many businesses have had to adapt to a fully remote model, which has been hard for some but has opened the doors to talent outside of the local area and to individuals who previously could not make it into an office.&#34; </p><p>It is still possible however that many of these roles will revert back to more physically-focused over time. </p><p>Hiring levels in the UK have surged as the economy unlocks following the COVID-19 lockdowns, rising by 92.6% in June compared to the same period last year, according to the survey.</p><p>In the US, job vacancies are also soaring, with the number of available positions rising to 9.21 million in May according to the Bureau of Labor Statistics&#39; <a href=\"https://www.bls.gov/jlt/\">Job Openings and Labor Turnover Survey</a>.</p><div class=\"read-original\">Read the original article on <a Jones)","articleImgCdnMap":{"https://i.insider.com/60eee920a8d8c00019b0312d?format=jpeg":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx8/cdn86@2020_4/2021/07/14/17-34-03-191_92f5ac1667f2c004.webp","http://feeds.feedburner.com/~ff/businessinsider?d=yIl2AUoC8zA":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx13/cdn5@2020_2/2021/07/14/17-34-04-185_cc3ef43fc8ff5801.webp","http://feeds.feedburner.com/~ff/businessinsider?i=nAt2L6eLFuE:fvE-JXpFL0A:F7zBnMyn0Lo":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx16/cdn63@2020_3/2021/07/14/17-34-01-912_d0bfefb80921ea82.webp","http://feeds.feedburner.com/~ff/businessinsider?i=nAt2L6eLFuE:fvE-JXpFL0A:V_sGLiPBpWU":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx11/cdn13@2020_4/2021/07/14/17-34-00-749_d972f28bf37d5c29.webp","http://feeds.feedburner.com/~ff/businessinsider?d=qj6IDK7rITs":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx14/cdn85@2020_2/2021/07/14/17-34-02-502_740defb435ea442b.webp","http://feeds.feedburner.com/~ff/businessinsider?i=nAt2L6eLFuE:fvE-JXpFL0A:gIN9vFwOqvQ":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx10/cdn98@2020_1/2021/07/14/17-34-04-861_05431e924299b6ce.webp","http://feeds.feedburner.com/~r/businessinsider/~4/nAt2L6eLFuE":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx27/cdn6@2020_2/2021/07/14/17-34-02-547_85d52708a3d5a768.webp"},"publishedOrCreatedDate":1626284019902},{"createdTime":"2021-07-15 01:33:39","updatedTime":"2021-07-15 01:33:39","title":"Student-loan companies aren't prepared to restart payments in October, which could be a 'financial catastrophe' for borrowers, senators say","link":"https://www.businessinsider.com/student-loan-companies-debt-payment-pause-extension-elizabeth-warren-2021-7","description":"<figure>\n\t<img src=\"https://i.insider.com/603d420087d37600190d076d?format=jpeg\" alt=\"Elizabeth Warren wearing a red blazer speaking at a microphone with a US flag visible behind her.\" height=\"1989\" width=\"3978\" charset=\"\">\n<figcaption>Sen. Elizabeth Warren.\n<p class=\"copyright\">Drew Angerer/Getty Images</p>\n</figcaption>\n</figure><ul class=\"summary-list\">\n<li>Elizabeth Warren asked student-loan servicers last month how they were preparing borrowers to restart payments.</li>\n<li>The servicers said they needed more time, calling the transition into repayment &#34;unprecedented.&#34;</li>\n<li>Lawmakers and advocates have called on Biden to extend the payment freeze through next year.</li>\n<li id=\"recirc\"><a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/?hprecirc-bullet\">See more stories on Insider&#39;s business page</a>.</li>\n</ul><p>The resumption of student-loan payments on October 1 is quickly approaching as borrowers, lawmakers, and advocates sound the alarm on restarting payments too early.</p><p>As it turns out, the companies that collect the payments aren&#39;t ready either.</p><p>Last month, Sens. Elizabeth Warren of Massachusetts, Ed Markey of Massachusetts, and Tina Smith of Minnesota <a href=\"https://www.warren.senate.gov/imo/media/doc/2021.06.21%20Letter%20to%20Navient%20re%20Restarting%20Student%20Loan%20Repayments.pdf\">sent a letter</a> to the CEOs of all student-loan servicers to request information on <a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/student-loan-servicers-restarting-payments-elizabeth-warren-debt-cancellation-navient-2021-6\">how each was preparing to transition borrowers back into repayment</a>.</p><p>On Tuesday, Warren and Markey released the responses from those servicers. The overarching theme was that servicers, along with borrowers, had concerns about restarting payments in just three months, the senators said.</p><p>&#34;The responses to our inquiry indicate that neither student loan borrowers nor student loan servicers are prepared for payments to resume, and servicers will need significant time to ensure that staffing and procedures are ready to provide borrowers with a high level of support,&#34; the senators wrote in a <a href=\"https://www.warren.senate.gov/imo/media/doc/2021.07.13%20Letter%20to%20Biden%20re%20servicer%20responses%20and%20payment%20pause%20extension.pdf\">letter</a> to President Joe Biden.</p><p>They said that one servicer even noted in its response that attempting to move over 43 million borrowers back into repayment at once was &#34;unprecedented.&#34;</p><p>Other main findings from the responses included:</p><ul><li>The payment pause had provided significant relief to borrowers, with 2.5 million having fully repaid their loans during the pandemic;</li><li>Most borrowers had very little contact with their servicers during the pandemic, suggesting they wouldn&#39;t be adequately prepared to restart payments;</li><li>Servicers needed more time to ensure staffing is sufficient to support borrowers;</li><li>And transitioning borrowers from FedLoan Servicing, which recently announced <a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/public-service-student-loan-forgiveness-pheaa-elizabeth-warren-2021-7\">it would not extend its contract</a> with the Education Department, would require additional time to ensure that borrowers are not harmed in the process.</li></ul><p>Last week, the Pennsylvania Higher Education Assistance Agency notified the department that it would not extend its 12-year contract for FedLoan Servicing, which handles the loans of 8.5 million borrowers, beyond December 14. Warren and Markey wrote in their letter that attempting to restart payments only weeks after transferring servicers would &#34;overwhelm an already broken student loan system.&#34;</p><p>On June 23, <a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/student-loan-debt-payment-pause-extensionelizabeth-warren-chuck-schumer-2021-6\" data-analytics-module=\"body_link\" data-analytics-post-depth=\"60\" data-uri=\"3c67f4bcfbaab17fd044b303d9920d2f\">64 Democrats</a>, led by Senate Majority Leader Chuck Schumer and Warren, urged Biden in a <a href=\"https://www.warren.senate.gov/imo/media/doc/Letter%20to%20Biden%20re%20extension%20of%20payment%20pause%20final%206.23.21.pdf\">letter</a> to extend the payment pause until March 31 or until the economy returns to pre-pandemic employment levels, whichever is longer.</p><p>The next day, <a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/student-loan-payment-pause-aclu-seiu-elizabeth-warren-debt-cancellation-2021-6\" data-analytics-module=\"body_link\" data-analytics-post-depth=\"80\" data-uri=\"67058cc076b22c5aa386d55b53901ee9\">128 organizations</a> including the American Civil Liberties Union and the Service Employees International Union sent a letter urging the president to extend the payment pause until the administration has followed through on its promises to fix the student-loan system and cancel federal student debt.</p><p>And in a letter on June 30, Sen. Patty Murray and Rep. Bobby Scott, the chairs of the Senate&#39;s and the House&#39;s education committees, <a href=\"https://www.help.senate.gov/imo/media/doc/2021-06-30%20Letter%20to%20Pres.%20Biden%20Payment%20Pause%20Extension.pdf\" data-analytics-module=\"body_link\" data-analytics-post-depth=\"80\" data-uri=\"8c603992e9fc6a8bd168586c39e96148\">urged Biden to extend the payment pause</a> until early 2022 to ensure that borrowers have the information they need to restart payments.</p><p>Education Department officials have also <a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/extend-pause-on-student-loan-payments-ends-september-2021-7\">reportedly urged Biden to extend the payment pause</a>. While Education Secretary Miguel Cardona has not said whether such an extension will happen, he has <a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/student-loan-payment-freeze-biden-education-secretary-cardona-debt-cancelation-2021-5\">hinted</a> at the <a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/biden-education-secretary-miguel-cardona-student-loan-payments-october-2021-6\">possibility</a> that it could.</p><p>&#34;As the economy recovers from this unprecedented crisis, borrowers should not be faced with an administrative and financial catastrophe just as they are beginning to regain their footing,&#34; Warren and Markey wrote. &#34;We strongly urge you to extend the pause on student loan interest and payments in order to allow time to begin to repair the broken student loan system.&#34;</p><div class=\"read-original\">Read the original 01:33:39","updatedTime":"2021-07-15 01:33:39","title":"Space-transport SPAC Momentus hit with $8 million SEC fine after misleading investors over propulsion technology","link":"https://www.businessinsider.com/spac-fraud-space-sec-momentus-gary-gensler-stable-road-2021-07","description":"<figure>\n\t<img src=\"https://i.insider.com/60eef85461b8600019f17033?format=jpeg\" alt=\"FILE PHOTO: The U.S. Securities and Exchange Commission logo adorns an office door at the SEC headquarters in Washington, June 24, 2011.   REUTERS/Jonathan Ernst\" height=\"1851\" width=\"3704\" charset=\"\">\n<figcaption>FILE PHOTO: SEC\n<p class=\"copyright\">Reuters</p>\n</figcaption>\n</figure><ul class=\"summary-list\">\n<li>The SEC announced charges on Tuesday against parties involved in a SPAC deal to take a space-flight company public. </li>\n<li>A $1.2 billion SPAC deal sought to merge with Momentus, a private start-up working on transporting satellites into space.</li>\n<li>But a test mission yielded &#34;no data to suggest that that thruster would deliver an impulse of any commercial significance.&#34;</li>\n<li id=\"recirc\"><a href=\"https://newsletter.businessinsider.com/join/4np/10-things-opening-bell\"><strong data-stringify-type=\"bold\">Sign up here for our daily newsletter, 10 Things Before the Opening Bell</strong><strong data-stringify-type=\"bold\">.</strong></a></li>\n</ul><p>The SEC on Tuesday announced charges against parties involved in a $1.2 billion space-transport SPAC for defrauding investors and obscuring the CEO&#39;s status as a national security risk.</p><p>&#34;This case illustrates risks inherent to SPAC transactions, as those who stand to earn significant profits from a SPAC merger may conduct inadequate due diligence and mislead investors,&#34; said SEC Chair Gary Gensler in a statement.</p><p>The SPAC, Stable Road Acquisition Corp, had sought to merge with Momentus, a private start-up, wit the intention of taking it public. Momentus&#39;s key offering was a &#34;microwave electro-thermal water plasma thruster,&#34; a way of zapping water vapor to propel a spacecraft, with the aim of transporting satellites into space.</p><p>But Momentus&#39;s propulsion tech failed to show results, according to SEC <a href=\"https://www.sec.gov/litigation/complaints/2021/comp-pr2021-124.pdf\">filings</a>. A test mission fell well short of the company&#39;s own benchmarks, and a former Momentus employee said that the test yielded &#34;no data to suggest that that thruster would deliver an impulse of any commercial significance.&#34;</p><p>That didn&#39;t stop the company&#39;s CEO, Mikhail Kokorich, from boasting of its successes.</p><p>&#34;Water plasma propulsion is now technologically mature enough to be baselined for operational in-space transportation missions,&#34; he told a trade publication in 2019, citing the Momentus test flight.</p><p>Meanwhile, Kokorich, who is a Russian citizen, had caught the eye of US authorities. CFIUS, a government body that scrutinizes foreign investment, flagged Kokorich as a national security threat, denying him permits and requiring him to divest from Momentus. </p><p>Kokorich&#39;s work visa was revoked. He applied for political asylum as a Russian dissident, but was denied. When the FBI and other agencies showed up at Momentus HQ to question employees, Kokorich was detained at an immigration detention center, though he was let go on bond.</p><p>Little of this was disclosed to investors. Despite Momentus disclosing in filings that it was &#34;highly dependent&#34; on Kokorich personally, he did not reveal his asylum application had been rejected. His presence at the company also prevented Momentus from getting crucial permits approved, according to the SEC.</p><p>The SEC is pursuing litigation against Kokorich in federal court, while all other parties have settled for a total penalty of $8 million. The <a href=\"https://www.ft.com/content/99de2333-e53a-4084-8780-2ba9766c70b7\">$1.2 billion</a> SPAC deal could still go ahead, though the SEC is requiring that the company let investors pull out freely.</p><div class=\"read-original\">Read the original article on <a href='https://www.businessinsider.com/spac-fraud-space-sec-momentus-gary-gensler-stable-road-2021-07'>Business valuation is unsustainable and new investors will get hurt.</li>\n<li id=\"recirc\"><a href=\"https://newsletter.businessinsider.com/join/4np/10-things-opening-bell?utm_source=markets&utm_medium=ingest?utm_source=markets&utm_medium=ingest?utm_source=markets&utm_medium=ingest?utm_source=markets&utm_medium=ingest?utm_source=markets&utm_medium=ingest?utm_source=markets&utm_medium=ingest?utm_source=markets&utm_medium=ingest?utm_source=markets&utm_medium=ingest?utm_source=markets&utm_medium=ingest?utm_source=markets&utm_medium=ingest?utm_source=markets&utm_medium=ingest?utm_source=markets&utm_medium=ingest?utm_source=markets&utm_medium=ingestdium=ingest?utm_source=markets&#38;utm_medium=ingest\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener\"><strong>Sign up here for our daily newsletter, 10 Things Before the Opening Bell.</strong></a></li>\n</ul><p><a href=\"https://markets.businessinsider.com/stocks/otly-stock\">Oatly</a> fell 6.1% to an all-time low of $19.40 Wednesday as short seller Spruce Point Capital Management accused the oat milk company of misleading investors on multiple fronts and overstating its revenue. <br><br>In a <a href=\"https://www.sprucepointcap.com/oatly-group-ab/\">report</a> published Wednesday, Spruce Point Capital Management said there is a long-term potential Oatly faces insolvency. </p><p>&#34;While investors are enamored with its sales growth in the plant-based food fad, and its commitment to ESG practices, we believe they should be focused on its loss of market share in Sweden and the U.S., minimal barriers to entry, lack of competitive advantages, rising commodity input costs, and supply challenges created partly through poorly planned production facilities,&#34; Spruce Point said. &#34;As such, we believe Oatly will sorely disappoint investors and will never achieve profitability.&#34;  <br><br>The short seller accused Oatly of shady accounting practices, claiming that the oat milk company has overstated its revenue and gross margin by 640 basis points. Spruce Point warned investors that Oatly has churned through three auditors in six years, and its CFO and audit chair were both involved in prior corporate accounting scandals. </p><p>In addition, Spruce Point said Oatly&#39;s nearly $12 billion valuation is unsustainable and will only hurt new investors. <br><br>&#34;Oatly&#39;s valuation has mysteriously ballooned nearly 6x since a $200m investment by Blackstone in July 2020 despite our evidence pointing to market share loss. Oatly is trading at 17x &#39;21E sales and 75x adjusted gross profit and a $12bn valuation (57% of the 2025 total projected non-dairy milk market),&#34; the short seller said. <br><br>Spruce Point is calling for Oatly&#39;s board to hire an independent forensic accountant to open an investigation the short seller&#39;s claims. </p><p>The short seller also blasted Oatly&#39;s ESG commitment, specifically the company&#39;s claims that its conversion from cow&#39;s milk to oat milk results in 80% fewer carbon emissions, 79% less land usage, and 60% less energy usage.</p><p>Oatly emphasized the claims on one of its <a href=\"https://investors.oatly.com/static-files/0bfad979-62b9-4d3d-84aa-6b112ee5c41b\">first slides</a> in its June investor presentation, but the data was from a 2013 study that didn&#39;t account for Oatly&#39;s recent expansion into the US and Asia.</p><p>&#34;In addition, we believe Oatly has &#34;cherry-picked&#34; the study&#39;s results by failing to show that its impact on water consumption is worse than dairy milk,&#34; said the short seller. &#34;Through a FOIA request, we learned that Oatly&#39;s production process also generates dangerous volumes of wastewater that requires it to build its own treatment facilities.&#34; </p><p> </p><div class=\"read-original\">Read the original article on <a src=\"https://i.insider.com/60eeeeaf61b8600019f16fe9?format=jpeg\" alt=\"tim cook peace sign\" height=\"1994\" width=\"3988\" charset=\"\">\n<figcaption>Apple CEO Tim Cook.\n<p class=\"copyright\">Roy Rochlin/WireImage/Getty Images</p>\n</figcaption>\n</figure><ul class=\"summary-list\">\n<li>Tech stocks could rise by another 10% in the second half of 2021, Wedbush said Wednesday. </li>\n<li>Analyst Dan Ives sees cloud and cybersecurity stocks as benefiting from spending on products to ward off cyberthreats. </li>\n<li>Apple and Microsoft are among top picks in the sector. </li>\n<li id=\"recirc\"><a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/?hprecirc-bullet\">See more stories on Insider&#39;s business page</a>.</li>\n</ul><p>Tech stocks have rebounded sharply from the losses suffered earlier this year, and should charge even higher through the rest of this year, said Wedbush on Wednesday, attributing its view on upcoming earnings and forward guidance and its expectation of robust demand for cybersecurity and cloud-based products.  </p><p>The projection comes as the second-quarter earnings season gets underway this week. Wedbush analyst Dan Ives in a note said tech behemoth <a href=\"https://markets.businessinsider.com/stocks/aapl-stock\">Apple</a> remains its top pick among large-cap tech names and that it would be buyers of <a href=\"https://markets.businessinsider.com/stocks/msft-stock\">Microsoft</a> and <a href=\"https://markets.businessinsider.com/stocks/zs-stock\">Zscaler</a>, among others. Apple and Microsoft shares on Tuesday hit all-time highs. </p><p>&#34;We believe June results and guidance around the corner over the coming weeks will be another positive catalyst for tech stocks and result in further multiple expansion as we see tech stocks up another 10%+ in [the second half of 2021] reflecting this good news,&#34; Ives wrote. </p><p>So far this year, the <a href=\"https://markets.businessinsider.com/index/nasdaq_100\">Nasdaq 100 index</a>, which includes Wall Street&#39;s largest tech and non-financial stocks, has advanced by 15%, and the broader <a href=\"https://markets.businessinsider.com/index/nasdaq_composite\">Nasdaq Composite</a> has bulked up by nearly 14%. Tech stocks have bounced back after a sell-off in March that was largely triggered by a rapid surge in long-dated government bond yields, implying higher borrowing costs. Yields steepened on expectations of hotter inflation in the face of higher government spending and the reopening of the economy hit hard by the pandemic. </p><p>The 16 months since the pandemic slammed into the US have led to a push in demand for cloud, e-commerce, cybersecurity, and other technology products and services. &#34;However, we believe massive growth (and further multiple expansion) is still on the horizon with tech stocks and FAANG names underestimating this surge of demand for the next 2-3 years,&#34; Ives said. </p><p>Wedbush expects spending for cloud and cybersecurity technology to surge in an effort to protect systems from cyber threats like the May ransomware attack against Colonial Pipeline, the largest fuel pipeline operator in the US. Wedbush sees a $200 billion growth opportunity in cloud security alone over the next few years. <a href=\"https://markets.businessinsider.com/stocks/vrns-stock\">Varonis Systems</a> and Zscaler remain among top picks in Wedbush&#39;s cybersecurity coverage. </p><p>Wedbush also said heading into the second half of the year it would own secular winners in the FAANG space, with Apple its favorite name, and cloud names including Microsoft, voice recording and data security company <a href=\"https://markets.businessinsider.com/stocks/nice-stock\">Nice</a> and customer relationship management software maker <a href=\"https://markets.businessinsider.com/stocks/pega-stock\">Pegasystems</a>.</p><div class=\"read-original\">Read the original article on <a Sticky</bi-shortcode><p>I&#39;m a professional travel writer who has visited Mexico many times for work and leisure, both with and without kids. So, I&#39;m often the go-to resource for those looking for recommendations on places to stay in the country.</p><p>Even prior to the pandemic, I preferred to avoid heavily trafficked tourist regions in favor of more under-the-radar destinations (often nearby and easily accessible from those busier spots) that offered comparatively quieter beaches and peaceful resorts. </p><p>My favorite is Punta Mita, less than three hours by direct flight from L.A., and a short car ride from Puerto Vallarta. And it&#39;s hardly an outlier  -  areas like Mayakoba, Oaxaca, and Careyes are regions that may be well known among frequent travelers to Mexico, but less so with first-time or casual travelers. </p><p>Here, we rounded up several Mexican destinations that might not yet be on your radar but should be. </p><aside class=\"quick-tip headline-regular\"><p><strong>Every hotel in Mexico on our list was selected based on the following criteria: </strong></p><ol><li aria-level=\"1\">We considered top-rated hotels renowned for their guest experience, spacious rooms, value, location, service, and more.</li><li aria-level=\"1\">Hotels are located in regions throughout Mexico that may be lesser known to inexperienced visitors compared to busy cities like Mexico City, famous party hotspots like Cancun, or even once under-the-radar destinations like Tulum that are now ultra-popular among travelers.</li><li aria-level=\"1\">Each has a <a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/reviews/out?u=https%3A%2F%2Fwww.tripadvisor.com%2F\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noopener sponsored\">Trip Advisor</a> rating of &#34;Very Good&#34; or above with a substantial number of reviews and is highly rated on other trusted traveler platforms like Booking.com.</li><li aria-level=\"1\">We included a range of prices, from a budget-minded hotel beginning at $67, to five-star luxury that starts under $1,000. </li><li aria-level=\"1\">In addition to location, we selected properties with notable amenities like pools, restaurants, and other features such as proximity to Mexico&#39;s famous beaches or Mayan landmarks.</li><li aria-level=\"1\">Each hotel promotes rigorous COVID-19 policies and protocols to reassure and protect guests, which we&#39;ve noted.</li></ol></aside><h3><strong>Browse all the best hotels below, or jump to a specific area.</strong></h3><ul class=\"summary-list\"><li><a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/best-mexico-hotels-no-crowds#punta-mita-1\">The best hotels in Mexico in Punta Mita</a></li><li><a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/best-mexico-hotels-no-crowds#more-of-the-best-places-tropical-hotels-to-book-16\">More of the best tropical hotels</a></li></ul><h2>These are the best hotels in Mexico that aren&#39;t in tourist hot spots, sorted by region and price.</h2>\n<div id=\"slideshow\">\n\tPunta Mita\n\t\n\t<p>Punta Mita is located along Mexico's Pacific coast on the north end of Banderas Bay in the state of Nayarit. It's about 20 miles from Puerto Vallarta, accessed via a short car ride. The destination is actually a 1,500-acre private peninsula, a gated area that is home to the Four Seasons Punta Mita, St. Regis Punta Mita, and other posh properties.</p>\n\tFour Seasons Punta Mita\n\t<figure>\n\t<img src=\"https://i.insider.com/60eda6fbca74780018ae90ea?format=jpeg\" alt=\"The exterior and beachview of the Four Seasons Resort Punta Mita\" height=\"900\" width=\"1200\" charset=\"\">\n<figcaption>Four Seasons Punta Mita has endless options for lounging outdoors, with two beaches, pools, and a lazy river.\n<p class=\"copyright\">Four Seasons Resort Punta Mita</p>\n</figcaption>\n</figure>\n\t<h3><a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/reviews/out?u=https%3A%2F%2Fwww.booking.com%2Fhotel%2Fmx%2Ffour-seasons-resort-punta-mita.en-gb.html%3Fai\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noopener sponsored\">Book Four Seasons Punta Mita</a></h3><aside class=\"quick-tip headline-regular\"><p><strong>Category:</strong> Luxury</p><p><strong>Typical starting/peak prices:</strong> $1,040/$1,450</p><p><strong>Best for:</strong> Families, couples, groups of friends, business travelers</p><p><strong>On-site amenities:</strong> 2 beaches, pools, lazy river, spa, salon, golf, tennis, kids club, multiple dining options, on-property COVID testing for guests</p><p><strong>Pros:</strong> The service here is impeccable &#8212; attentive without being invasive, and highly personalized. The stunning beaches, pools, and lazy river all make for ideal places to lounge. The kids club programming is outstanding.</p><p><strong>Cons:</strong> The hotel's prices seemed to creep up following its sweeping multi-year, multimillion-dollar renovation. And while those updated offerings make it a fair trade, the price tag will be too steep for many.</p></aside><p>Easily accessed from the Puerto Vallarta airport (which is itself served by many airlines, including low-cost carriers with direct flights), the Four Seasons Punta Mita feels like another world.</p><p>There are two secluded beaches at this paradise, separated by a dramatic clifftop perch that makes an unforgettable private dinner destination for a special occasion. There's an adults-only pool and an infinity-edge all-ages pool, plus a serene lazy river that almost feels like it meanders naturally through a jungle.&#160;</p><p>There are multiple dining options including the sprawling Dos Catrinas restaurant that anchors the center of the resort. Bahia by Richard Sandoval is right on the sand, and Aramara serves upscale Asian fare.</p><p>Newly renovated rooms are out of this world with entry-level lodgings that come in at a sprawling 645 square feet of indoor-outdoor space with room for three adults or two adults and two kids, sophisticated beachy decor, and marble bathrooms.</p><p>As a parent traveling with young children, I can't say enough good things about the kids club here. It's like a luxurious summer camp that kids will never want to leave and comes included with the room rate, which makes for an outstanding value if you use it to its fullest.</p><p>Overall, this property is one of my favorites in the world for family travel and the place we've chosen for many major occasions and milestones.</p><p><strong>COVID-19 procedures are available</strong> <a href=\"https://www.fourseasons.com/puntamita/welcome-back/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener\">here</a>.</p>\n\tMayakoba\n\t\n\t<p>Just about 30 miles from Cancun is the 500-acre development of Mayakoba (technically in Playa del Carmen, though far more peaceful and remote).</p><p>Mayakoba encompasses 620 acres of lagoons, jungles, and beaches along Mexico's Riviera Maya. The private gated community is home to an array of full-service resorts, all designed with the goal of preserving and enhancing the native landscape. In addition to the Fairmont and Banyan Tree properties that made our list, other attractive options include Andaz, Viceroy, and Rosewood, which also come highly recommended.</p>\n\tFairmont Mayakoba\n\t<figure>\n\t<img src=\"https://i.insider.com/60edae2d61b8600019f16cbc?format=jpeg\" alt=\"The exterior of the Fairmont Mayakoba\" height=\"900\" width=\"1200\" charset=\"\">\n<figcaption>Fairmont Mayakoba offers golf, spa, beach, and pools across 45 acres.\n<p class=\"copyright\">Fairmont Mayakoba</p>\n</figcaption>\n</figure>\n\t<h3><a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/reviews/out?u=https%3A%2F%2Fwww.booking.com%2Fhotel%2Fmx%2Ffairmont-mayakoba.en-gb.html\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noopener sponsored\">Book Fairmont Mayakoba</a></h3><aside class=\"quick-tip headline-regular\"><p><strong>Category:</strong> Mid-range</p><p><strong>Typical starting/peak prices:</strong> $213/$379</p><p><strong>Best for:</strong> Families, couples, groups of friends, business travelers</p><p><strong>On-site amenities:</strong> El Camaleon golf course, spa, pools, restaurants, Discovery Kids Club, multiple dining options</p><p><strong>Pros:</strong> With its full-scale suite of amenities, this large resort is ideal for golf fans, spa enthusiasts, and families with kids. And it comes in at a more down-to-earth price point than some of the other more opulent properties within the Mayakoba development.&#160;</p><p><strong>Cons:</strong> Some critical recent reviews note that construction has caused noise and other disruptions.&#160;&#160;&#160;</p></aside><p>This 45-acre property is an enormous full-service resort offering 401 rooms and suites, including 34 suites with an array of beach and lagoon casitas. Standard guest rooms are generously sized at 436 to 480 square feet, with abundant natural light, a private terrace or balcony, and large spa-like bathrooms with marble accents and soaking tubs.</p><p>Book the property as an all-inclusive &#8212; or not as you prefer. Activities include nature trails, biking, kayaks, catamarans, tennis, golfing on the renowned El Camaleon golf course (host to the only official PGA Tour event in Mexico), and scenic boat tours through the canals.</p><p>Of course, lounging waterside is the main draw, with white sand beaches and several pools on property. The Willow Stream Spa offers signature Mayan treatments and the hotel is pet friendly and family friendly, with the Discovery Kids Club and a water slide at the main pool.</p><p>Dining options are so plentiful and woven throughout all the Mayakoba resorts. Take a complimentary town car ride to any of the other hotels where you can dine and still charge your meal to your room.&#160;</p><p><strong>COVID-19 procedures are available</strong> <a href=\"https://www.fairmont-mayakoba.com/blog/covid-19/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener\">here</a>.</p>\n\tBanyan Tree Mayakoba\n\t<figure>\n\t<img src=\"https://i.insider.com/60edc043ca74780018ae91a2?format=jpeg\" alt=\"The beachview of Banyan Tree Mayakoba in Mexico\" height=\"900\" width=\"1200\" charset=\"\">\n<figcaption>Banyan Tree Mayakoba is the only all-pool villa resort in the Riviera Maya.\n<p class=\"copyright\">Banyan Tree Mayakoba</p>\n</figcaption>\n</figure>\n\t<h3><a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/reviews/out?u=https%3A%2F%2Fwww.booking.com%2Fhotel%2Fmx%2Fbanyan-tree-mayankoba.en-gb.html\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noopener sponsored\">Book Banyan Tree Mayakoba</a></h3><aside class=\"quick-tip headline-regular\"><p><strong>Category:</strong> Luxury</p><p><strong>Typical starting/peak prices:</strong> $435/$952</p><p><strong>Best for:</strong> Couples, families, groups of friends, business travelers</p><p><strong>On-site amenities:</strong> Restaurants, spa, golf, pools, kids club, beach, complimentary COVID antigen testing</p><p><strong>Pros:</strong> This is among the most elite places to stay in Mayakoba, overlaying Asian-inspired service across a chic, eco-minded Mexican resort experience.</p><p><strong>Cons:</strong> Critical reviews question the value for the price tag.</p></aside><p>Banyan Tree Mayakoba bills itself as the most sustainable five-star resort in a region known for them. It recently underwent a $50 million expansion, debuting 34 private beachfront pool suites and the new Sands Beach Club, which has an infinity oceanfront pool, all-day dining restaurant and raw bar, beachfront lounge, a larger interactive Rangers Club for kids, and ocean view massage rooms operated by the Banyan Tree Spa.&#160;</p><p>Banyan Tree Mayakoba offers 120 villas, which all come with indulgent private pools and terraces. It's the only all-pool villa resort in the Riviera Maya. Even the smallest rooms among them clocks in around 1,700 square feet with high design and thoughtfully curated details such as included bicycles at each. While the resort is lavish and inviting, it's easy to spend your entire trip within your room, swimming in your own pool and spreading out on the various living spaces, with every need tended to by a butler.</p><p><strong>COVID-19 procedures are available</strong> <a href=\"https://www.banyantree.com/en/travel-advisory\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener\">here</a>.</p>\n\tOaxaca\n\t\n\t<p>Oaxaca is a state in southern Mexico steeped in historic architecture and indigenous culture. Its capital city of the same name is dotted with charming colonial buildings often made of green volcanic stone. The baroque Catedral de Oaxaca stands in the main square, El Z&#243;calo.&#160;</p>\n\tParador De Alcala\n\t<figure>\n\t<img src=\"https://i.insider.com/60edd341a8d8c00019b02ed9?format=jpeg\" alt=\"The streetview of the Hotel Parador de Alcalá\" height=\"900\" width=\"1200\" charset=\"\">\n<figcaption>Parador De Alcala is located in the heart of Oaxaca’s historic center.\n<p class=\"copyright\">Hotel Parador de Alcalá</p>\n</figcaption>\n</figure>\n\t<h3><a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/reviews/out?u=https%3A%2F%2Fwww.booking.com%2Fhotel%2Fmx%2Fparador-de-alcala.en-gb.html\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noopener sponsored\">Book Parador De Alcala</a></h3><aside class=\"quick-tip headline-regular\"><p><strong>Category:</strong> Budget</p><p><strong>Typical starting/peak prices:</strong> $67/$128</p><p><strong>Best for:</strong> Couples, business travelers&#160;</p><p><strong>On-site amenities:</strong> Pool with solarium, restaurant, business center, fitness center, meeting room</p><p><strong>Pros:</strong> This hotel has an unbeatable central location that is excellent for walkers, right in the heart of Oaxaca. The rooftop pool is another standout.&#160;</p><p><strong>Cons:</strong> There's no elevator here, and not every traveler will find it accessible. Critical reviewers found some rooms unremarkable.</p></aside><p>Parador De Alcala is a boutique hotel located in the heart of the historic center between the Santo Domingo de Guzm&#225;n Ex-convent and the Zocalo.</p><p>Here, 21 rooms and suites take over a restored and converted eighteenth-century mansion. The lodgings are distributed over three levels with high ceilings and most have access from a stunning colonial courtyard. All rooms have marble flooring, Egyptian cotton sheets, and a soft color palette highlighted by natural light.&#160;</p><p>El Patio restaurant is located in one of the hotel's central atrium spaces, offering full traditional Oaxacan breakfast. A terrace, garden, and chaises lounges surround the pool deck, which offers 360-degree views of the city.</p><p><strong>COVID-19 procedures are available</strong> <a href=\"https://paradordealcalaoaxaca.mx/limpioyseguro.php\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener\">here</a>.</p>\n\tNaNa Vida Hotel Boutique Oaxaca\n\t<figure>\n\t<img src=\"https://i.insider.com/60edd6c061b8600019f16db5?format=jpeg\" alt=\"A room in the NaNa Vida Hotel Boutique Oaxaca\" height=\"900\" width=\"1200\" charset=\"\">\n<figcaption>The boutique NaNa Vida is located in the heart of Oaxaca, ideal for sightseeing on foot.\n<p class=\"copyright\">NaNa Vida Hotel Boutique Oaxaca</p>\n</figcaption>\n</figure>\n\t<h3><a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/reviews/out?u=https%3A%2F%2Fwww.booking.com%2Fhotel%2Fmx%2Fnana-vida.en-gb.html%3F\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noopener sponsored\">Book NaNa Vida Hotel Boutique Oaxaca</a></h3><aside class=\"quick-tip headline-regular\"><p><strong>Category:</strong> Budget</p><p><strong>Typical starting/peak prices:</strong> $85/$108</p><p><strong>Best for:</strong> Families, couples, groups of friends.</p><p><strong>On-site amenities:</strong> Weekend breakfast and lighter weekday fare included, cantina with games, in-room massages, business center, tours and cooking classes&#160;</p><p><strong>Pros:</strong> NaNa Vida is an excellent value that is ideally situated for walkability around Oaxaca. The service is top-notch.</p><p><strong>Cons:</strong> Rooms are on the smaller side and may have spotty hot water since it is solar heated. Past guests have complained of noise bleed.</p></aside><p>NaNa Vida Hotel Oaxaca is situated right in the center of Oaxaca City, about 1,500 feet from Santo Domingo Convent, and steps from restaurants and bars for easy and relaxed sightseeing. The San Pablo Cultural Centre and Macedonio Alcal&#225; Theater are just blocks away.</p><p>Rooms are unique, artful, and stylishly outfitted, with colorful bedding and intricately patterned bathroom tiling. Many elements of the decor are made by local artisans.</p><p>You will not find a pool in this boutique property, but you can relax in the sunny courtyard and enjoy full breakfast on weekends (or pastries and coffee during the week). At a soap bar, guests can select their own scents for bespoke soaps, using 100 percent natural and vegan ingredients, for use during their stay.&#160;</p><p><strong>COVID-19 procedures are available</strong> <a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/reviews/out?u=https%3A%2F%2Fwww.tripadvisor.com%2FHotel_Review-g150801-d12352501-Reviews-NaNa_Vida_Hotel_Boutique_Oaxaca-Oaxaca_Southern_Mexico.html\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noopener sponsored\">here</a>.</p>\n\tCostalegre\n\t\n\t<p>Costalegre is a 150-mile long stretch of the Mexican coast on the Pacific within the state of Jalisco, between Puerto Vallarta and Manzanillo. It features an array of beaches, capes, and bays, plus charming seaside towns and villages.</p>\n\tEl Careyes Club & Residences\n\t<figure>\n\t<img src=\"https://i.insider.com/60edd8d061b8600019f16dc4?format=jpeg\" alt=\"Bird eye&#39;s view of the exterior of El Careyes Club &#38; Residences\" height=\"900\" width=\"1200\" charset=\"\">\n<figcaption>Careyes is a favorite among in-the-know travelers for its vibrant colors and artful installations.\n<p class=\"copyright\">Careyes</p>\n</figcaption>\n</figure>\n\t<h3><a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/reviews/out?u=https%3A%2F%2Fwww.booking.com%2Fhotel%2Fmx%2Fel-careyes.en-gb.html%3F\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noopener sponsored\">Book El Careyes Club &#38; Residences</a></h3><aside class=\"quick-tip headline-regular\"><p><strong>Category:</strong> Luxury</p><p><strong>Typical starting/peak prices:</strong> $338/$607</p><p><strong>Best for:</strong> Couples, families, groups of friends</p><p><strong>On-site amenities:</strong> Infinity pools, lighted tennis courts, restaurant dining, private access beach club</p><p><strong>Pros:</strong> Careyes is vividly colorful and full of unique, artful wonders including spiritual, sculptural structures known as \"Careyes Wonders\" that dot the property. Conscious travelers will love that the Careyes Foundation is deeply devoted to holistic development within the local community.</p><p><strong>Cons:</strong> Careyes is unlike a standard resort. It's eclectic, arty, and unique and that vibe may not be for travelers seeking the standard vacation fare.</p></aside><p>Careyes is the place you go when you are in the cognoscenti &#8230; or at least you'll certainly look like you are when you visit. Founded by Gian Franco Brignone in 1968, this unique resort has been continuously family-owned and operated since then, exuding a vibe that combines a sultry Mediterranean feel with the ultra-saturated colors and unique architecture of Mexico. Think eccentric, arty, and focused on wellness and the natural environment.</p><p>El Careyes has infinity pools, lighted tennis courts, restaurant dining, and a private access beach club. The resort is comprised of bungalows, casitas, villas, and so-called \"Ocean Castles,\" which are opulent, dreamy lodgings. Entry-level accommodations are brilliantly colored bungalows located directly on the sand overlooking the Careyes Bay just steps from the sea and beach club.</p><p>The property spans over 35,000 acres including the biosphere reserve. The so-called \"Careyes Wonders\" on-site include spiritual-feeling spaces that guests can visit (or book for events), including La Copa del Sol, an 88-foot diameter cup-like structure that is acoustically and visually arresting, and definitely sets this place apart.</p><p>Careyes also has a lively event calendar, including the chicer-than-Burning-Man, Ondalinda Festival.&#160;</p><p><strong>COVID-19 procedures are available</strong> <a href=\"https://www.careyes.com/covid19\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noopener sponsored\">here</a>.</p>\n\tTequila\n\t\n\t<p>This town is located in the western state of Jalisco. It's famous for &#8212; of course &#8212; the production of the famous Mexican spirit. Located near the Tequila Volcano, its outskirts are awash in fields of the main ingredient in the spirit: blue agave. An array of local distilleries and haciendas offer tours of the production (and tastings too, of course).</p>\n\tCasa Salles\n\t<figure>\n\t<img src=\"https://i.insider.com/60edddc2a8d8c00019b02f23?format=jpeg\" alt=\"The Casa Salles Hotel Boutique building\" height=\"900\" width=\"1200\" charset=\"\">\n<figcaption>The boutique Casa Salles has 25 intimate guest rooms.\n<p class=\"copyright\">Casa Salles</p>\n</figcaption>\n</figure>\n\t<h3><a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/reviews/out?u=https%3A%2F%2Fwww.booking.com%2Fhotel%2Fmx%2Fcasa-salles-boutique-tequila.en-gb.html\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noopener sponsored\">Book Casa Salles</a></h3><aside class=\"quick-tip headline-regular\"><p><strong>Category:</strong> Boutique</p><p><strong>Typical starting/peak prices:</strong> $136/$163</p><p><strong>Best for:</strong> Families, couples, groups of friends</p><p><strong>On-site amenities:</strong> Restaurant, spa, pool</p><p><strong>Pros:</strong> The service, food, and understated elegance within this new boutique hotel earn high praise. The distillery tour is a highlight of staying here.&#160;</p><p><strong>Cons:</strong> This 25-room property offers a boutique experience, which won't suit travelers looking for the vibe and offerings of a sprawling resort.</p></aside><p>Casa Salles Hotel Boutique opened in Tequila in 2020. The site that had been used for Salles family celebrations over the past 60 years is now a destination with 25 intimate guest rooms. Located within walking distance of the town square and other tourist landmarks, Casa Salles Hotel Boutique is an ideal launchpad.</p><p>Guest rooms are thoughtfully appointed with built-in furnishings, private bars, seating areas, smart TVs, and rainfall showers. Large Master Family Suites have room for seven adults, with sliding glass doors that open to private balconies overlooking a picturesque mango grove and gardens.</p><p>The hotel also offers a lively restaurant, Mango Cocina de Origen, serving regional Mexican cuisine. There's also a pool, banquet facility, and spa, and the La Guarre&#241;a Distillery, producer of El Tequile&#241;o tequila, is located adjacent to the hotel.</p><p><strong>COVID-19 procedures are available</strong> <a href=\"https://www.casasalles.com/covid-19-information\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noopener sponsored\">here</a>.</p>\n\tMérida\n\t\n\t<p>This is the lively capital of the Yucat&#225;n, the peninsula state that separates the Gulf of Mexico from the Caribbean Sea, and is also home to Cancun and Playa Del Carmen.</p><p>Rich in Maya and colonial history, the city's centerpiece is the Plaza de la Independencia, bordered by the colonial-era churches M&#233;rida Cathedral and Iglesia de la Tercera Orden, both built with relics from ancient Mayan temples.</p>\n\tThe Diplomat Merida\n\t<figure>\n\t<img src=\"https://i.insider.com/60ede0de61b8600019f16df1?format=jpeg\" alt=\"A seating area in The Diplomat Merida\" height=\"900\" width=\"1200\" charset=\"\">\n<figcaption>The Diplomat Merida is hip and stylish, with colonial architecture and a beautiful pool.\n<p class=\"copyright\">The Diplomat Merida</p>\n</figcaption>\n</figure>\n\t<h3><a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/reviews/out?u=https%3A%2F%2Fwww.booking.com%2Fhotel%2Fmx%2Fthe-diplomat-hotel.en-gb.html\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noopener sponsored\">Book The Diplomat Merida</a></h3><aside class=\"quick-tip headline-regular\"><p><strong>Category:</strong> Boutique</p><p><strong>Typical starting/peak prices:</strong> $135/$295</p><p><strong>Best for:</strong> Couples, groups of friends</p><p><strong>On-site amenities:</strong> Pool, breakfast, welcome drinks</p><p><strong>Pros:</strong> Guests love that this hotel is so well located for exploring M&#233;rida. The pool and ultra-personalized service get high marks.</p><p><strong>Cons:</strong> Once more of a hidden gem, this hotel has gotten tons of attention in prestigious travel media &#8212; so the secret is out.</p></aside><p>The hip, stylish Diplomat is well situated in the city's historic center, within easy walking distance of many historic monuments, cathedrals, and parks, plus tons of eateries and shops. The hotel boasts colonial architecture and a beautiful pool.</p><p>Entry-level suites are high on style and comfort with colonial tiles, smart TVs, sound docks, included high-speed Wi-Fi, Nespresso machine, fans, premium linens, and air conditioning.</p><p>Snacks and fresh cocktails are served on arrival, and an ever-changing vegetarian breakfast is also included and served daily. Guests have access to a tea and coffee bar with fresh juices and champagne in the morning, as well.</p><p><strong>COVID-19 procedures are available</strong> <a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/reviews/out?u=https%3A%2F%2Fwww.tripadvisor.com%2FHotel_Review-g150811-d6208752-Reviews-The_Diplomat_Boutique_Hotel-Merida_Yucatan_Peninsula.html\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noopener sponsored\">here</a>.</p>\n\tFAQ: Mexico hotels\n\t\n\t<h2>When is the best time to visit Mexico?</h2><p>The weather differs by region across the country, but generally, September through May is a good time to visit Mexico.</p><p>Mexico gets much of its rain throughout the summer, but these may be quick and isolated showers that won't derail a trip.</p><p>The Gulf of Mexico area sees hurricanes from late July through early November. It's hottest in April and May, and the busiest seasons are during the Christmas holiday and spring break periods.&#160;</p><h2>What is the best Mexico hotel on the beach to avoid crowds?&#160;</h2><p>Secluded beaches dot the country's coastline. The island of Holbox is a small 26-mile island within the protected YUM Balam nature reserve and offers pristine, crowd-free beaches, enjoyed by hotels like <a href=\"https://www.villasflamingos.com/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener\">Villas Flamingos</a> or the <a href=\"https://www.mystiqueresorts.com/resort/mystique-blue\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener\">Mystique Holbox</a> by Royalton.</p><p>Elsewhere, Four Seasons Punta Mita has the advantage of being located a short drive from Puerto Vallarta airport, but boasts a pair of very quiet beaches all to itself.</p><h2>Can I drink the water in Mexico?</h2><p>It's generally not a good idea to drink water from the tap in Mexico. Opt instead for bottled water, even while brushing your teeth. Be mindful of ice and avoid getting it in your drinks unless you can confirm it's made from safe water.&#160;</p><h2>Is it safe to stay in a hotel?</h2><p>While hotels do provide opportunities for face-to-face interactions with staff and other guests in common spaces like check-in desks, lobbies, and dining venues, <a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/are-hotels-safe-coronavirus\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener\">experts say guests who exercise proper precautions</a> can stay safely in hotels.</p><p>However, no travel is completely risk-free right now and we recommend following CDC current guidelines as well as all applicable local protocols at the time of travel.</p><h2>Is Mexico safe for U.S. travelers?</h2><p><a href=\"https://wwwnc.cdc.gov/travel/notices/covid-3/coronavirus-mexico\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener\">CDC advises</a> that unvaccinated travelers should avoid nonessential travel to Mexico. It currently lists Mexico as a Level 3 (out of 4) COVID level. See the CDC's <a href=\"https://wwwnc.cdc.gov/travel/notices/covid-3/coronavirus-mexico#vax\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener\">recommendations for fully vaccinated travelers</a> and <a href=\"https://wwwnc.cdc.gov/travel/notices/covid-3/coronavirus-mexico#unvax\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener\">recommendations for unvaccinated travelers</a>. Travelers should follow recommendations or requirements in Mexico, including wearing a mask and staying six feet apart from others.</p><h2>What are the best Mexico hotels for couples or families?</h2><p>As a parent of young children, I'll always pick a Four Seasons anywhere in the world for top-notch service that accommodates families indulgently and seamlessly, with included kids clubs and incredible all-seasons programming. So, the Four Seasons Punta Mita is my go-to pick in Mexico for families.</p><p>And while many of Mexico's most well-known adults-only resorts for couples are located in popular destinations like Cancun, couples seeking romance might find it a treat to visit a hotel like Casa Salles in less-frequently visited Tequila, where spirits tasting makes for memorable, grown-folks-only fun.</p>\n\tMore law","link":"https://www.businessinsider.com/companies-with-forced-labor-ties-xinjiang-china-legal-risks-us-2021-7","description":"<figure>\n\t<img src=\"https://i.insider.com/60eefee861b8600019f1705f?format=jpeg\" alt=\"Security guards stand at the gates of what is officially known as a vocational skills education centre in Huocheng County\" height=\"2400\" width=\"3199\" charset=\"\">\n<figcaption>Security guards stand at the gates of what is officially known as a vocational skills education centre in Huocheng County.\n<p class=\"copyright\">Thomas Peter/Reuters</p>\n</figcaption>\n</figure><ul class=\"summary-list\">\n<li>The US warned that companies with investment or supply-chain ties to Xinjiang can face legal risks.</li>\n<li>China has been accused of committing genocide and crimes against humanity in Xinjiang.</li>\n<li>Major US companies have been accused of sourcing cotton and product components in the region.</li>\n<li id=\"recirc\"><a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/?hprecirc-bullet\">See more stories on Insider&#39;s business page</a>.</li>\n</ul><p>The US on Tuesday cautioned that companies that invest, provide venture capital, or have supply-chain ties to the Xinjiang region of China <a href=\"https://www.state.gov/wp-content/uploads/2021/07/Xinjiang-Business-Advisory-13July2021-1.pdf\">&#34;run a high risk of violating U.S. law,&#34;</a> due to widespread reports of forced labor and other human rights violations against ethnic minorities in the region.</p><p>The US has accused China of committing genocide and crimes against humanity in Xinjiang, citing the arbitrary mass detention of mostly Muslim ethnic groups in the region in what the Chinese government calls &#34;re-education camps.&#34; The government has also <a href=\"https://www.bbc.com/news/world-asia-china-22278037\">forcibly sterilized, tortured, and sexually abused ethnic minority prisoners</a> in these camps, according to former detainees. </p><p>Companies who don&#39;t pull out of the region could violate statutes that criminalize benefitting from or importing goods that are the result of forced labor. The advisory also warned US companies against assisting in the development of surveillance tools for Xinjiang or supplying US-made goods to entities that use forced labor.</p><p>In 2020, activist groups accused some of the world&#39;s biggest fashion brands - including Nike and H&#38;M - of <a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/uighur-forced-labor-global-brands-profited-activists-letter-2020-7\">sourcing cotton from factories that exploit the forced labor of Uyghurs</a> and other ethnic minorities. Over a million ethnic minorities have been detained in Xinjiang, a region that produces a fifth of world&#39;s cotton, and activist groups have called for companies to exit the region to avoid profiting from human rights violations in the area. </p><p>Nike <a href=\"https://purpose.nike.com/statement-on-xinjiang\">stated that it doesn&#39;t source products, textiles and yarn</a> from Xinjiang, and H&#38;M stated that it was <a href=\"https://www.voanews.com/east-asia-pacific/voa-news-china/hm-vows-regain-customers-after-backlash-over-uyghur-comments\">concerned about the accusations of forced labor</a> involved in Xinjiang cotton production.</p><p>In May, <a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/apple-china-suppliers-uyghur-muslims-forced-labor-report-2021-5\">Apple suppliers were linked to forced labor in the Xinjiang region</a>, with reports that thousands of detained Uyghurs were used to manufacture components for Apple devices. Apple previously <a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/apple-china-suppliers-uyghur-muslims-forced-labor-report-2021-5\">denied exploiting forced labor</a> in Xinjiang.</p><p>In 2020, Apple and Nike, among other companies, also <a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/apple-nike-coca-cola-lobbied-china-uyghur-forced-labor-bill-2020-11\">lobbied to weaken the Uyghur Forced Labor Prevention Act</a> that would ban US companies from importing goods made in Xinjiang unless they could prove they weren&#39;t made with forced labor. </p><p>According to Reuters, the <a href=\"https://www.reuters.com/world/us/us-state-department-warns-business-risk-linked-chinas-xinjiang-2021-07-13/\">US may impose additional sanctions on China</a> and may extend a similar business advisory to Hong Kong.</p><div class=\"read-original\">Read the original article on <a
